(@p3, @p4, @p5, 1),
(@p6, @p7, @p8, 2),
(@p9, @p10, @p11, 3),

SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[LoanTemplateName], [t].[Status], [t].[Id0], [t1].[Id], [t1].[Title], [t1].[Id0], [t1].[Key], [t1].[Title0], [t1].[Value], [t1].[Id00], [t1].[Type], [t1].[OptionsUrl], [t1].[SectionId], [t1].[Calculated], [t1].[Options], [t1].[Readonly], [t1].[Validation]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l].[Id], [l].[LoanTemplateName], [l].[Status], [l0].[Id] AS [Id0]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l]
    INNER JOIN [LoanTemplates] AS [l0] ON [l].[LoanTemplateId] = [l0].[Id]
    WHERE [l].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[Title], [t0].[Id] AS [Id0], [t0].[Key], [t0].[Title] AS [Title0], [t0].[Value], [t0].[Id0] AS [Id00], [t0].[Type], [t0].[OptionsUrl], [t0].[SectionId], [t0].[Calculated], [t0].[Options], [t0].[Readonly], [t0].[Validation], [s].[LoanTemplateId]
    FROM [Sections] AS [s]
    OUTER APPLY (
        SELECT [f0].[Id], [f0].[Key], [f0].[Title], [f].[Value], [f].[Id] AS [Id0], [f0].[Type], [f0].[OptionsUrl], [f0].[SectionId], [f0].[Calculated], [f0].[Options], [f0].[Readonly], [f0].[Validation]
        FROM [FieldValues] AS [f]
        INNER JOIN [Fields] AS [f0] ON [f].[FieldId] = [f0].[Id]
        WHERE [l].[Id] = [f].[LoanId]
    ) AS [t0]
) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id0] = [t1].[LoanTemplateId]
